# Window

- Category: XML Element Type
- Confidence level: HIGH
- Confidence score: 100/100

## Confidence Assessment

- Level: HIGH

- Final score: 100/100

- Raw weighted score: 135

- Rationale: Promoted as HIGH confidence because matches default ui or extracted base ui surface, seen in 4 or more addons, used directly in xml handler attributes.

## Evidence Signals

- +30 Seen in 4 or more addons: Cross-addon spread is strong.
- +35 Matches default UI or extracted base UI surface: Symbol aligns with known default-interface namespaces.
- +30 Used directly in XML handler attributes: XML exposure suggests an engine-level contract.
- +25 Matches a known engine namespace: Namespace shape matches WAR engine APIs.
- +15 Role is consistent across addons: The same symbol serves the same kind of job across addons.

## Description

Window is the primary XML container element for addon UI frames. It commonly hosts named child elements and binds lifecycle or input events to Lua handlers.

## Common Attributes

- alpha
- handleinput
- id
- inherits
- layer
- movable
- name
- popable
- savesettings
- scale
- skipinput
- sticky

### Per-Event Lua API Calls

**OnLButtonUp** handlers call: `AnimatedImageStartAnimation`, `BroadcastEvent`, `ButtonGetDisabledFlag`, `ButtonGetPressedFlag`, `ButtonSetDisabledFlag`, `ButtonSetPressedFlag`, `DestroyWindow`, `DynamicImageSetTexture`, `LabelGetText`, `LabelSetTextColor`, `ListBoxGetDataIndex`, `SliderBarSetCurrentPosition`, `SliderBarSetDisabledFlag`, `SystemData.ActiveWindow.name:match`, `SystemData.ActiveWindow.name:sub`, `SystemData.MouseOverWindow.name:match`, `WindowGetAnchor`, `WindowGetId`, `WindowGetMovable`, `WindowGetParent`, `WindowGetScale`, `WindowGetShowing`, `WindowSetAlpha`, `WindowSetGameActionData`, `WindowSetMovable`, `WindowSetShowing`, `WindowUtils.ToggleShowing`

**OnMouseOver** handlers call: `DoesWindowExist`, `DynamicImageSetTexture`, `LabelSetText`, `LabelSetTextColor`, `SystemData.ActiveWindow.name:find`, `SystemData.ActiveWindow.name:match`, `SystemData.ActiveWindow.name:sub`, `SystemData.MouseOverWindow.name:match`, `SystemData.MouseOverWindow.name:match:gsub`, `WindowGetAlpha`, `WindowGetDimensions`, `WindowGetId`, `WindowGetParent`, `WindowGetScale`, `WindowGetScreenPosition`, `WindowSetAlpha`, `WindowSetDimensions`, `WindowSetScale`, `WindowSetShowing`, `WindowSetTintColor`, `WindowStartAlphaAnimation`, `WindowUtils.OnMouseOverButton`

**OnHidden** handlers call: `BroadcastEvent`, `ButtonGetPressedFlag`, `ButtonSetDisabledFlag`, `ButtonSetText`, `ComboBoxSetDisabledFlag`, `ComboBoxSetSelectedMenuItem`, `DoesWindowExist`, `DynamicImageSetTexture`, `LabelSetText`, `SliderBarSetCurrentPosition`, `TextEditBoxSetText`, `UnregisterEventHandler`, `WindowGetDimensions`, `WindowGetShowing`, `WindowGetTintColor`, `WindowSetDimensions`, `WindowSetShowing`, `WindowSetTintColor`, `WindowStartAlphaAnimation`, `WindowStopAlphaAnimation`, `WindowUtils.OnHidden`, `WindowUtils.RemoveFromOpenList`

**OnInitialize** handlers call: `ButtonSetCheckButtonFlag`, `ButtonSetPressedFlag`, `ButtonSetText`, `ButtonSetTextColor`, `ComboBoxAddMenuItem`, `ComboBoxSetSelectedMenuItem`, `CreateWindow`, `CreateWindowFromTemplate`, `DoesWindowExist`, `DynamicImageSetTexture`, `DynamicImageSetTextureDimensions`, `LabelSetText`, `LabelSetTextColor`, `Player.CancelSpell`, `RegisterEventHandler`, `TextEditBoxSetText`, `UnregisterEventHandler`, `WindowGetId`, `WindowGetScale`, `WindowGetShowing`, `WindowRegisterCoreEventHandler`, `WindowRegisterEventHandler`, `WindowSetAlpha`, `WindowSetGameActionData`, `WindowSetGameActionTrigger`, `WindowSetShowing`, `WindowSetTintColor`, `WindowUtils.EscapeKeyProcessed`

**OnRButtonUp** handlers call: `ButtonGetPressedFlag`, `ButtonSetPressedFlag`, `ButtonSetText`, `ComboBoxSetSelectedMenuItem`, `CreateWindow`, `DestroyWindow`, `DoesWindowExist`, `LabelSetText`, `LabelSetTextColor`, `SliderBarSetCurrentPosition`, `SystemData.ActiveWindow.name:match`, `SystemData.ActiveWindow.name:sub`, `SystemData.MouseOverWindow.name:match`, `SystemData.MouseOverWindow.name:match:gsub`, `TextEditBoxSetText`, `WindowAddAnchor`, `WindowClearAnchors`, `WindowGetId`, `WindowGetMovable`, `WindowGetParent`, `WindowSetAlpha`, `WindowSetMovable`, `WindowSetShowing`, `WindowStopAlphaAnimation`, `WindowUtils.ToggleShowing`

**OnShown** handlers call: `BroadcastEvent`, `ButtonSetPressedFlag`, `ButtonSetText`, `ComboBoxSetDisabledFlag`, `CreateWindowFromTemplate`, `DoesWindowExist`, `LabelSetText`, `RegisterEventHandler`, `TextEditBoxSetText`, `WindowAddAnchor`, `WindowAssignFocus`, `WindowClearAnchors`, `WindowGetAlpha`, `WindowGetDimensions`, `WindowGetShowing`, `WindowSetDimensions`, `WindowSetShowing`, `WindowSetTintColor`, `WindowStartAlphaAnimation`, `WindowStopAlphaAnimation`, `WindowUtils.AddToOpenList`, `WindowUtils.OnShown`

**OnLButtonDown** handlers call: `BroadcastEvent`, `ButtonSetPressedFlag`, `LabelGetText`, `LabelSetTextColor`, `SystemData.ActiveWindow.name:match`, `SystemData.MouseOverWindow.name:find`, `SystemData.MouseOverWindow.name:match`, `SystemData.MouseOverWindow.name:sub`, `WindowAddAnchor`, `WindowClearAnchors`, `WindowGetId`, `WindowGetParent`, `WindowGetScreenPosition`, `WindowGetShowing`, `WindowSetAlpha`, `WindowSetDimensions`, `WindowSetGameActionData`, `WindowSetShowing`, `WindowSetTintColor`

**OnMouseOverEnd** handlers call: `DoesWindowExist`, `DynamicImageSetTexture`, `LabelSetText`, `LabelSetTextColor`, `SystemData.MouseOverWindow.name:match`, `WindowGetParent`, `WindowSetAlpha`, `WindowSetShowing`, `WindowSetTintColor`, `WindowStartAlphaAnimation`

**OnShutdown** handlers call: `DestroyWindow`, `DoesWindowExist`, `UnregisterEventHandler`, `WindowAddAnchor`, `WindowGetDimensions`, `WindowGetShowing`, `WindowSetDimensions`, `WindowSetShowing`

**OnRButtonDown** handlers call: `SystemData.ActiveWindow.name:match`, `SystemData.MouseOverWindow.name:find`, `SystemData.MouseOverWindow.name:match`, `SystemData.MouseOverWindow.name:sub`, `WindowGetId`, `WindowSetShowing`, `WindowSetTintColor`

**OnUpdate** handlers call: `BroadcastEvent`, `ButtonGetDisabledFlag`, `ButtonSetHighlightFlag`, `DynamicImageSetRotation`, `LabelGetText`, `LabelSetText`, `WindowGetAlpha`, `WindowGetDimensions`, `WindowGetScreenPosition`, `WindowGetShowing`, `WindowSetAlpha`, `WindowSetGameActionData`, `WindowSetShowing`, `WindowSetTintColor`, `WindowStartAlphaAnimation`

**OnKeyEscape** handlers call: `ButtonSetPressedFlag`, `DestroyWindow`, `DoesWindowExist`, `TextEditBoxGetText`, `WindowAssignFocus`, `WindowGetId`, `WindowGetShowing`, `WindowSetShowing`

**OnMButtonUp** handlers call: `WindowGetShowing`

**OnMButtonDown** handlers call: `WindowSetShowing`

**OnSizeUpdated** handlers call: `WindowGetDimensions`, `WindowSetDimensions`

**OnInitializeCustomSettings** handlers call: `WindowSetScale`

**OnSetMoving** handlers call: `WindowGetShowing`

- AbilityAlert: AAWindow -> Window AAWindow
